***идиот.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:идиот.html>идиот</a> (2657)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1803. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">idiōta</i> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">idiot</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Idiot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἰδιώτης</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">idiṓtēs</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a private citizen, one who has no professional knowledge, layman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идиот.html>идио́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">idiót</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идиот.html>идио́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идиот.html>идио́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идиот.html>идио́тов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идиотка.html>идио́тка</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>idiot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:идиот.html>идио́т</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ty takój <b>idiót</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You're such an <b>idiot</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***идиотский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:идиотский.html>идио́тский</a> (6848)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идиот.html>идио́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">idiót</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идиотский.html>идио́тский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">idiótskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>idiotic</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ди.html>ди</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>о́т</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ский</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3a✕~.

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">אידיש</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">idish</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, alternative form of <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">ייִדיש</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yidish</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Language names that are nouns form their adverbs with the preposition <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (+ prepositional case), rather than with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. For example: <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:идиш.html>и́дише</a></b></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na <b>ídiše</b></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in <b>Yiddish</b></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>..</li></ul>

***идол.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:идол.html>и́дол</a> (11692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">идолъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">idolŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εἴδωλον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">eídōlon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">image, idol</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идол.html>и́дол</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ídol</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идол.html>и́дола</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идол.html>и́долы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идол.html>и́долов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>idol</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> callous person</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и́</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:дол.html>дол</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***идти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> (96)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The infinitive spelled with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">д</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">d</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is attested since the 14th century, under influence of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>иду́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">idú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёшь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">idjóšʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, etc.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">idtí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойти́</a></b>) <i>(concrete verbs)</i>
</p>
<ol><li>to go
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>Идём</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кинотеатр.html>кинотеа́тр</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Idjóm</b> v kinoteátr!</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Let's go</b> to the movie theater!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to walk</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of precipitation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>Идёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождь</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Idjót</b> doždʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It’s raining.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>Идёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снег</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Idjót</b> sneg.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It’s snowing.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>Идёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>град</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Idjót</b> grad.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It’s hailing.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to function, to work
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>иду́т</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éti časý ne <b>idút</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This clock/watch doesn't <b>work</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to suit, to become <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of wearing clothes</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:костюм.html>костю́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Étot kostjúm jemú <b>idjót</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This suit suits him.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">used in expressions</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vrémja <b>idjót</b> býstro.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Time flies.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:куда.html>куда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>шло́</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto ješčó kudá ni <b>šlo</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That's still all right. (colloquial)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:товар.html>това́ры</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>иду́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ix továry <b>idút</b> xorošó.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Their products <b>are selling</b> well.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>О</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чём</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>речь</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">O čóm <b>idjót</b> rečʹ?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What is being talked about? / What is it all about? / What is the topic? / What are you guys talking about?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>Речь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>двух</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>трёх</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вещь.html>веща́х</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Rečʹ <b>idjót</b> o dvux/trjóx veščáx.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">[insert subject] is/are talking about two/three things.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Всё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>пла́ну</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vsjó <b>idjót</b> po plánu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Everything <b>is going</b> as planned.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>Во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:передача.html>переда́ча</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vo skólʹko <b>idjót</b> éta peredáča?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What time <b>is</b> this (television) program <b>on</b>?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнение.html>сравне́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> че́м-либо/ке́м-либо.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto ne <b>idjót</b> ni v kakóje sravnénije s čém-libo/kém-libo.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It cannot be compared with something/someone.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:компромисс.html>компроми́сс</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>idtí</b> na kompromíss</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to compromise, make a compromise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уступка.html>усту́пки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">idtí na ustúpki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to compromise, make concessions</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:риск.html>риск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">idtí na risk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run a risk, take a chance</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">idtí na vsjó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be ready to do anything, go to any length</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пята.html>пята́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">idtí po pjatám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to follow in someone's footsteps; to follow on the heels of</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>Идти́</a></b> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pojtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are Russian concrete verbs. Their counterpart, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is an abstract verb.</li>
<li>Prefixed derivatives of this verb are formed using the combining form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-йти́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:иды.html>и́д</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,   <a href = vnd.unilang:изолированный.html>изоли́рованное</a> спряжение, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — ^b/b(9).     <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существовать.html>существу́ют</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:устаревший.html>устаре́вшие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> деепр. <a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>наст</a>. вр.: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>иду́чи</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> прош. вр.: <i>ше́д</i>. См. <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойти́</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="устаревшее">устар.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a>: итти. <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> 1956 <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>года</a></span>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-ид-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ти</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***иероглиф.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иероглиф.html>иеро́глиф</a> (12207)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иероглиф.html>иеро́глиф</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ijeróglif</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иероглиф.html>иеро́глифа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иероглиф.html>иеро́глифы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иероглиф.html>иеро́глифов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hieroglyph</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> undecipherable handwriting, inscrutable symbol</li>
<li>Chinese character (hanzi), usually "<a href = vnd.unilang:китайский.html>кита́йский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иероглиф.html>иеро́глиф</a>". See also: ханьцзы.</li></ol>

***иже.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иже.html>и́же</a> (26730)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:иже.html>и́же</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iže</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иже.html>и́же</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">íže</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ecclesiastic or literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> which; et cetera</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>In modern Russian, the inflections are not preserved and various forms are perceived as independent</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:иже.html>и́же</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iže</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иже.html>и́же</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">íže</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>izhe, name of the Cyrillic (Old Church Slavonic) letter і, ї</li></ol>

***из.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> (21)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*eǵʰs</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁eǵʰs</i>.
</p>

***изба.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изба.html>изба́</a> (1870)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">изъба, истъба</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izŭba, istŭba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьstъba</i>, which may be related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stubō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">room, sitting room, oven</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or to <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">étuve</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heated room, bathroom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*extupāre</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изба.html>изба́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izbá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изба.html>избы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изба.html>и́збы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изба.html>изб</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>izba, (peasant's) log hut, cottage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выносить.html>выноси́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сор.html>сор</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изба.html>избы́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vynosítʹ sor iz <b>izbý</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wash one’s dirty linen in public</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:избавитель.html>избави́тель</a> (20763)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избавить.html>изба́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izbávitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to redeem, rescue, save</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">er</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избавитель.html>избави́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izbavítelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избавитель.html>избави́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избавитель.html>избави́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избавитель.html>избави́телей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">избави́тельница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>redeemer, rescuer, savior</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ба.html>ба</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ви́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тель</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 2a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избегнуть.html>избе́гнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izbégnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избегать.html>избега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izbegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избежать.html>избежа́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избегнуть.html>избе́гнуть</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive or infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to avoid, to evade, to elude</li>
<li>to refrain from</li>
<li>to keep off, to steer clear, to shun</li>
<li>to escape <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from trouble, misfortune, punishment, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:обежать.html>обежа́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:обегать.html>обе́гать</a></li>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства_2"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>га́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.     <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>Есть</a> страд. <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:избегнуть.html>избе́гнуть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:избежать.html>избежа́ть</a>.
<a href = vnd.unilang:участник.html>Уча́стники</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ситуация.html>ситуа́ции</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:описываемый.html>опи́сываемой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощью</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:избегать.html>избега́ть</a></i>: <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:субъект.html>субъект</a> (им. п.), <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:объект.html>объект</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>. п. <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> неопр. <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> гл.).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>из-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-бег-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:избегнуть.html>избе́гнуть</a> (28550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бе́гнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-bégnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избегнуть.html>избе́гнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izbégnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избегать.html>избега́ть</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive or infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to avoid, to evade, to elude</li>
<li>to refrain from</li>
<li>to keep off, to steer clear, to shun</li>
<li>to escape <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from trouble, misfortune, punishment, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
